[30;1m235 | [0m[35m========================[0m
[30;1m236 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m237 | [0m[35mThe password file is a simple newline separated list of ``:`` separated fields. It[0m
[30;1m238 | [0m[35mis located at ``$HOME/.pgpass`` for most systems and at[0m
[30;1m239 | [0m[35m``%APPDATA%\postgresql\pgpass.conf`` for Windows based systems. However, the[0m
[30;1m240 | [0m[35m``PGPASSFILE`` environment variable may be used to override that location.[0m
